function trans(str) {
var langList = ['en','en','zh','fr','de','ja','es'],
langType = top.document.getElementById('langType').value;
langType = !!langList[langType] ? langList[langType] : 'en';
if (langType === 'en') {
return str;
if (lang[str]) {
return lang[str][langType];
} else {
return str;

function checkIPv4Address(field)
var obj=field.value;
var exp=/^(\d{1,2}|1\d\d|2[0-4]\d|25[0-5])\.(\d{1,2}|1\d\d|2[0-4]\d|25[0-5])\.(\d{1,2}|1\d\d|2[0-4]\d|25[0-5])\.(\d{1,2}|1\d\d|2[0-4]\d|25[0-5])$/;
var reg = obj.match(exp);
if(reg==null)
return false;
else
return true;
function CreateButtons(type,butname,fntn,btnid,optn)
butname = trans(butname);
if((optn == "off") ||(optn == ""))
str = "<input type='"+type+"' class='buttonsOff' name='"+btnid+"' id='"+btnid+"' value='"+butname+"' onclick='"+fntn+"'>";
else if(optn == "on")
str = "<input type='"+type+"' class='buttonsOn'  id='"+btnid+"' name='"+btnid+"' title='"+butname+"' value='"+butname+"' onclick='"+fntn+"'>";
return str;

hr{margin-left:10px;margin-right:0px;color:#e7e5e4;}function showHelpWindowAndTitle (name, windowOrTitle)
	var strHelp = null;
	var strTitle = null;
	switch (name)
		case "switchInformation":
			strHelp = "help_switch_info.html#switchInfo";
			strTitle = "Switch Information Help";
			break;
		case "changePassword":
		       strHelp = "help_reset.html#changePassword";
			strTitle = "Maintenance Help";
			break;
		case "plusUtility":
			strHelp = "help_plus_utility.html#plusUtility";
			strTitle = "Switch Management Mode Help";
			break;
		 case "ipSource":
			strHelp = "help_access_control.html#ipSource";
			strTitle = "Access Control Help";
			break;
		 case "igmpSnoopingConf":
			strHelp = "help_igmp_snooping.html#igmpSnooping";
			strTitle = "IGMP Snooping Help";
			break;
		case "loopDetection":
			strHelp = "help_loop_detection.html#loopDetection";
			strTitle = "Loop Detection Help";
			break;
		case "portStatus":
			strHelp = "help_port_status.html#portStatus";
			strTitle = "Port Status Help";
			break;
		case "portMirroring":
			strHelp = "help_port_mirroring.html#portMirroring";
			strTitle = "Port Mirroring Help";
			break;
		case "cableTester":
			strHelp = "help_cable_tester.html#cableTester";
			strTitle = "Cable Tester Help";
			break;
		case "QosGlobalConfQos":
			strHelp = "help_qos.html#qosCfg";
			strTitle = "Quality of Service Help";
			break;
		case "QosGlobalConfPort":
			strHelp = "help_qos.html#portPri";
			strTitle = "Port Priority Help";
			break;
		case "basicPortVlanStatus":
			strHelp = "help_portBased_basic_vlan.html#basicPortVlanStatus";
			strTitle = "Basic Port-based VLAN Help";
			break;
		case "basicPortVlanGroup":
			strHelp = "help_portBased_basic_vlan.html#basicPortVlanGroup";
			strTitle = "Basic Port-based VLAN Help";
			break;
		case "advancePortVlanStatus":
			strHelp = "help_portBased_advance_vlan.html#advancePortVlanStatus";
			strTitle = "Advaced Port-based VLAN Help";
			break;
		case "advancePortVlanConfig":
			strHelp = "help_portBased_advance_vlan.html#advancePortVlanConfig";
			strTitle = "Advaced Port-based VLAN Help";
			break;
		case "advancePortVlanMember":
			strHelp = "help_portBased_advance_vlan.html#advancePortVlanMember";
			strTitle = "Advaced Port-based VLAN Help";
			break;
		case "basic8021qVlanStatus":
			strHelp = "help_8021q_basic_vlan.html#basic8021qVlanStatus";
			strTitle = "Basic 802.1Q VLAN Help";
			break;
		case "basic8021qVlanId":
			strHelp = "help_8021q_basic_vlan.html#basic8021qVlanId";
			strTitle = "Basic 802.1Q VLAN Help";
			break;
		case "advance8021qVlanStatus":
			strHelp = "help_8021q_advance_vlan.html#advance8021qVlanStatus";
			strTitle = "Advaced 802.1Q VLAN Help";
			break;
		case "advance8021qVlanId":
			strHelp = "help_8021q_advance_vlan.html#advance8021qVlanId";
			strTitle = "Advaced 802.1Q VLAN Help";
			break;
		case "advance8021qVlanMember":
			strHelp = "help_8021q_advance_vlan.html#advance8021qVlanMember";
			strTitle = "Advaced 802.1Q VLAN Help";
			break;
		case "advance8021qPvid":
			strHelp = "help_8021q_advance_vlan.html#advance8021qPvid";
			strTitle = "Advaced 802.1Q VLAN Help";
			break;
		case "rateLimit":
			strHelp = "help_rate_limit.html#rateLimit";
			strTitle = "Rate Limit Help";
			break;
		case "broadcastFiltering":
			strHelp = "help_broadcast_filtering.html#broadcastFiltering";
			strTitle = "Broadcast Filtering Help";
			break;
		default:
			if(windowOrTitle == 0) alert ('Help page ' + name + ' not found');
			break;
	if(windowOrTitle == 0)
		strHelp = (strHelp == null) ? "error" : strHelp;
		document.getElementById ('maincontent').contentWindow.location.replace (strHelp);
	else if(strTitle != null)
		document.write("<span>&nbsp;</span>");
function showWinTitle(name)
  showHelpWindowAndTitle(name, 1);
function showHelpwindow (name)
  showHelpWindowAndTitle(name, 0);
<!DOCTYPE HTML>
<html>
<head>
<meta http-equiv="Pragma" content="no-cache">
<meta http-equiv="Content-Type" content="text/html; charset=UTF-8">
<title>Help for VLAN</title>
<link rel=stylesheet href="/help.css?z4" type="text/css">
<script  src="/frame.js?z4"></script>
</head>
<body>
<h1><a name="advance8021qVlanStatus"></a>Help for Advance 802.1Q VLAN Status</h1>
<ul>
  <li withsubtag>Advanced 802.1Q VLAN Status - Click <b>Enable</b> or <b>Disable</b> to set the Advanced 802.1Q VLAN Status. Note: The current VLAN settings are lost if the status is changed.</li>
</ul>
<hr size=1 align="center"> 
<h1><a name="advance8021qVlanId"></a>Help for Advanced 802.1Q VLAN Identifier Setting</h1>
<ul>
<li>VLAN ID - Specify the VLAN Identifier for the new VLAN. The range of the VLAN ID is 1 to 4094. User can create a maximum of 64 VLANs.</li>
<li>Port Members - The ports that are included in the VLAN.</li>
<li>Add - Add a new VLAN to the switch.</li>
<li>Delete - Delete selected VLANs from the switch.</li>
</ul>
<hr size=1 align="center"> 
<h1><a name="advance8021qVlanMember"></a>Help for VLAN Membership</h1>
<ul>
  <li>VLAN ID - Select the VLAN ID for which you want to display or configure.</li>
  <li>Group Operation - This field allows you to apply the same operation on all ports.
  		<ul>
  			<li>Untag All - Select all the ports to be included in this VLAN where all frames transmitted will be untagged.</li>
  			<li>Tag All - Select all the ports to be included in this VLAN where all frames transmitted will be tagged.</li>
  			<li>Remove All - Remove all ports from the selected VLAN.</li>
  		</ul>
	</li>
  <li>Ports - You can use this port list to add or remove port member to the selected VLAN. Each port has three modes:
  		<ul>
			<li>T(Tagged) - All frames transmitted from this port will be tagged with selected VLAN ID.</li>
			<li>U(Untagged) -  All frames transmitted from this port will not be tagged with VLAN ID.</li>
			<li>Blank - This port is not a member of the selected VLAN.</li>
  		</ul>
 </li>
</ul>
<hr size=1 align="center"> 
<h1><a name="advance8021qPvid"></a>Help for PVID Configuration</h1>
<ul>
  <li>Port - The port you want to configure.</li>
  <li>PVID - Specify the VLAN ID you want assigned to untagged or priority tagged frames received on this port. The factory default is 1.</li>
</ul>
</body>
</html>

<h1><a name="basic8021qVlanStatus"></a>Help for Basic 802.1Q VLAN Status</h1>
<ul>
  <li withsubtag>Basic 802.1Q VLAN Status - Click <b>Enable</b> or <b>Disable</b> to set the Basic 802.1Q VLAN Status. Click the <b>Apply</b> button. Note: The current VLAN settings are lost if the status is changed.</li>
</ul>
<hr size=1 align="center"> 
<h1><a name="basic8021qVlanId"></a>Help for Basic 802.1Q VLAN Identifier</h1>
<ul>
  <li withsubtag>VLAN ID - Under each port to be added to a VLAN, enter the VLAN ID of the VLAN. You can enter a VLAN ID from 1 to 4093 or <b>all</b>. VLAN group ID <b>all</b> means that this is the port that you want to use for all existing VLANs. Note: If ports are members of the same LAG, you must assign them to the same VLAN.</li>
</ul>
</body>

<h1><a name=ipSource></a>Help for Access Control</h1>
<ul>
<li>Access control allows access to the switch by a single or range of specified IP addresses by mask. Use 255.255.255.255 as the mask for a single specified IP address.</li>
</ul>

<link rel=stylesheet href="/help.css?z4" type="text/css">
<script  src="/frame.js?z4"></script>

<body>
<h1><a name="broadcastFiltering"></a>Help for Broadcast Filtering</h1>
<ul>
<li>Broadcast Filtering - You can configure the switch to block broadcast storms (massive transmission of broadcast packets forwarded to every port on the same VLAN). If they are not blocked, broadcast storm packets can delay or halt the transmission of other data. When you turn on broadcast filtering, you have the option to set the storm control rate on each port of your switch.</li>
</ul>
</body>
</html>

<title>Help for Cable Tester</title>
<link rel=stylesheet href="/help.css?z4" type="text/css">
<script  src="/frame.js?z4"></script>
</head>
<body>
<h1><a name=cableTester></a>Help for Cable Tester</h1>
<p>You can use the cable diagnostic feature to easily find out the health status of network cables.
If any problems exist, this feature helps quickly locate the point where the cabling fails, allowing connectivity issues to be fixed much faster, potentially saving technicians hours of troubleshooting. 
If an error is detected, the distance at which the fault is detected is stated in meters.(This is the distance from the port.) The cable length reported by the test may have a tolerance.</p>
<ul>
<li>Test Results - Indicates the test results of the cable. Possible results are:
	<ul type="square">
        <li>Crosstalk: There is an interpair short on the cable.</li>
        <li>Failed: An error occurred while conducting the cable test. Try again.</li>
        <li>No Cable: The cable does not exist or the cable length is too small to test accurately.</li>
        <li>Not Supported: The test is not supported on this port.</li>
        <li>Mismatch:  There is a mismatch with the cable impedance. Replace the Ethernet cable, and then try again.</li>
        <li>OK: The cable is working correctly.</li>
        <li>Open Cable: The cable is disconnected or there is a faulty connection.</li>
        <li>Short: There is an electrical short in the cable.</li>
        <li>Open short: Both disconnect and electrical short are detected in the cable.</li>
      </ul>
</li> 
<li>Cable Fault Distance - Indicates the distance (in meter) from the failed point on the cable.</li>
</ul>
</body>

<body>
<h1><a name=powerSavingMode></a>Help for Power Saving Mode</h1>
<p>Click Enable or Disable to turn on or off all of the power saving methods for the device.</p>
<ul>
<li>The Energy Efficient Ethernet (EEE) - Supports operation in Low Power Idle (LPI) mode. When LPI mode is enabled, systems on both sides of the link can disable portions of their functionality and save power during periods of low link utilization.</li>
<li>Link-Down Power Saving - Reduces the power consumption considerably when the network cable is disconnected. When the network cable is reconnected, the switch detects an incoming signal and restores normal power.</li>
<li>Short Cable Power Saving - Dynamically detects and adjusts power that is required for the detected cable length.</li> 
</ul>                  
</body>

<!DOCTYPE HTML>
<html>
<head>
<meta http-equiv="Pragma" content="no-cache">
<meta http-equiv="Content-Type" content="text/html; charset=UTF-8">
<title>Help for IGMP Snooping</title>
<link rel=stylesheet href="/help.css?z4" type="text/css">
<script  src="/frame.js?z4"></script>
</head>
<body>
<h1><a name=igmpSnooping></a>Help for IGMP Snooping</h1>
<p>Internet Group Management Protocol (IGMP) snooping allows a switch to forward multicast traffic intelligently on the switch.
Multicast IP traffic is traffic that is destined to a host group.</p>
<p>IGMP host groups' IP addresses range from 224.0.0.0 to 239.255.255.255. Based on the IGMP query and report messages, the switch forwards traffic only to the ports that request the multicast traffic. This feature prevents the switch from broadcasting the traffic to all ports and possibly affecting network performance.</p>
<ul>
<li withsubtag>IGMP Snooping Status - Click <b>Enable</b> or <b>Disable</b> to configure the IGMP Snooping Status.</li>
<li>VLAN ID Enabled for IGMP Snooping - Enter a valid VLAN ID to enable IGMP snooping for the VLAN. This field is dimmed if VLAN is not enabled.</li>
<li withsubtag>Validate IGMPv3 IP header - Click <b>Enable</b> or <b>Disable</b> to configure the IGMPv3 IP Header option. When the Validate IGMPv3 IP header option is enabled, IGMPv3 messages are required to have TTL = 1, ToS Byte = 0xC0 (Internetwork Control), and the router alert IP option (9404) set.</li>
<li withsubtag>Block Unknown Multicast Address - Click <b>Enable</b> or <b>Disable</b> to configure the Block Unknown Multicast Address option. When this feature is enabled, instead of flooding, all unknown multicast packets are dropped.</li>
<li>IGMP Snooping Static Router Port - Select a port as the dedicated IGMP snooping static router port.
After a port is selected as the static router port, all IGMP Join and Leave reports are forwarded to it.
If you select Any in this field, IGMP Join and Leave packets are sent to every port of the switch.</li>
</ul>
</body>

<h1><a name=loopDetection></a>Help for Loop Detection</h1>
<p>Loop detection is a feature that determines whether or not a loop exists. If the switch detects a loop, both LED lights blink at a constant speed. Loop status is cleared if no loop is detected after approximately 16 seconds.</p>
</body>
</html><!DOCTYPE HTML>
<html>

<body>
<h1><a name="plusUtility"></a>Help for Switch Management Mode</h1>
<ul>
<li>Web browser Only - You cannot manage the switch using the Plus Utility. The switch and its IP address on the network are still discoverable through the Plus Utility. This is the default selection.</li>
<li>Web browser and Plus Utility - You will be able to manage the switch using both the web browser and the Plus Utility.</li>
</ul>
</body>

<!DOCTYPE HTML>

<head>

<title>Help for VLAN</title>
<link rel=stylesheet href="/help.css?z4" type="text/css">
<script  src="/frame.js?z4"></script>
</head>
<body>
<h1><a name="advancePortVlanStatus"></a>Help for Advanced Port-Based VLAN Status</h1>
<p>In an advanced port-based VLAN configuration, you can assign a single port to multiple VLANs. By default, all ports are members of VLAN 1.</p>
<ul>
  <li withsubtag>Advanced Port-based VLAN Status - Click <b>Enable</b> or <b>Disable</b> to set the Advanced Port-based VLAN Status. Click the <b>Apply</b> button. Note: The current VLAN settings are lost if the status is changed.</li>
</ul>
<hr size=1 align="center"> 
<h1><a name="advancePortVlanConfig"></a>Help for VLAN Configuration</h1>
<ul>
  <li>VLAN Identifier - Select the VLAN ID for which you want to display or configure data. VLAN IDs are limited to the number of ports on the switch.</li>
  <li>Group Operation - This field allows you to select or remove all ports for this VLAN.</li>
  <li>Port List - Select or unselect the port(s) you want for the VLAN.</li>
</ul>
<hr size=1 align="center"> 
<h1><a name="advancePortVlanMember"></a>Help for VLAN Membership</h1>
<ul>
  <li>VLAN ID - The VLAN Identifier (VID) of the VLAN. The range of VLAN ID is 1 to the total of port numbers.</li>
  <li>Port Members - The ports that are included in the VLAN.</li>
</ul>
</body>
</html>

<html>
<head>

<body>
<h1><a name="basicPortVlanStatus"></a>Help for Basic Port-Based VLAN Status</h1>
<P>The Basic Port Based VLAN Configuration page lets you partition your network into different segments. Ports with the same VLAN ID are grouped into the same VLAN group.</P>
<ul>
  <li withsubtag>Basic Port-based VLAN Status - Click <b>Enable</b> or <b>Disable</b> to set the Basic Port-based VLAN Status. Click the <b>Apply</b> button. Note: The current VLAN settings are lost if the status is changed.</li>
</ul>
<hr size=1 align="center"> 
<h1><a name="basicPortVlanGroup"></a>Help for Basic Port-based VLAN Group</h1>
<ul>
  <li withsubtag>VLAN Group - You can enter a VLAN ID from 1 to 5. If all the VLANs share an uplink to the Internet or servers, enter <b>all</b> in the VLAN ID field for the port that you want to use for the uplink. Note: If ports are members of the same LAG, you must assign them to the same VLAN.</li>
</ul>
</body>
</html>

<link rel=stylesheet href="/help.css?z4" type="text/css">
<script  src="/frame.js?z4"></script>
</head>
<body>
<h1><a name="portMirroring"></a>Help for Port Mirroring</h1>
<ul>
<li>Source Port - You can select more than one source port. Traffic from the source port is sent to the destination port. You cannot select a source port that is a member of a LAG.</li>
<li>Destination Port - You can select a single destination port only. The destination port receives all traffic from the mirror ports. You cannot select a destination port that is a member of a LAG.</li>
</ul>                    
</body>
</html>

<link rel=stylesheet href="/help.css?z4" type="text/css">
<script  src="/frame.js?z4"></script>

<body>
<h1><a name="portStatus"></a>Help for Port Status</h1>
<ul>
<li>Auto Negotiation -  The port negotiates with the link partner and works out speed, duplex operation, and flow control. This is the default setting. 
When auto-negotiation is disabled, port speed, duplex operation, and flow control is programmable by the user.</li>
<li>Flow Control - Flow control works by pausing a port if the port becomes oversubscribed and dropping all traffic for small bursts of time during the congestion condition.You can enable or disable the IEEE 802.3x flow control.</li>
</ul>                    
</body>

<link rel=stylesheet href="/help.css?z4" type="text/css">
<script  src="/frame.js?z4"></script>
</head>
<body>
<h1><a name="qosCfg"></a>Help for Quality of Service</h1>
<p>Quality of Service is a means of providing consistent, predictable data delivery by distinguishing packets with strict timing requirements from those that are more tolerant of delay. If Port Based mode is selected, the packet priority is based on the port priority configuration. If 802.1p/DSCP Based mode is selected, the switch forwards packet according to 802.1p tag or DSCP tag. If an ingress packet has both 802.1p and DSCP tags, 802.1p will take precedence over DSCP, the switch forwards packet according to 802.1p tag.</p>
<hr size=1 align="center">
<h1><a name="portPri"></a>Help for Port Priority</h1>
<p>A Port Priority is available in Port Based Mode. Each port can be assigned to one of the four priorities:
to high: Low Priority, Normal Priority, Medium Priority and High Priority.</p>
</body>

<body>
<h1><a name="rateLimit"></a>Help for Rate Control Setting</h1>
<ul>
<li>Ingress Rate - Use the pull-down menu to select an Ingress rate limit. Packets will be dropped if the rate of the incoming packets is beyond the selected rate limit. The default value is No Limit.</li>
<li>Egress Rate - Use the pull-down menu to select an Egress rate limit.Packets will be dropped if the transmitting rate is beyond the selected rate limit.The default value is No Limit.</li>
</ul>
</body>
</html>

<h1><a name="changePassword"></a>Help for Change Password</h1>
<ul>
  <li>New Password - Enter the new password. Password must be 6-20 characters, and contain at least one uppercase letter, one lowercase letter, and one numeral. Allowed symbols are !@#$%^&*()</li>
</ul>
</body>

<h1><a name="switchInfo"></a>Help for Switch Information</h1>
<ul>
<li>Switch Name - Enter the name of this switch. The name can contain up to 20 alpha-numeric characters. Only a-z, A-Z, 0-9, and the following symbols are allowed: ~!@#$%^&*()_+=-`{}][":';/.,?><\|.</li>
<li>DHCP Mode - Enable the DHCP mode to use dynamic IP address for the switch. Disable to enter static IP address.</li>
</ul>
</body>

          document.getElementById('netmask').disabled = false;

          document.getElementById('gateway').disabled = false;

          document.getElementById('netmask').disabled = true;
          document.getElementById('gateway').disabled = true;

<script type="text/javascript">
var timer;
function RegistrationCheck()
        return false;
    var serviceURL = "https://my.netgear.com/Registration/deviceping.aspx?callback=JsonpProcess&serial=%s";
    if(sessionStorage.getItem("%u") === "%u")
    {
    }
    var script = document.createElement('script');
    script.setAttribute('src', serviceURL);
    // load the script
    document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
    timer = setTimeout("ShowErrMsg()",60000);
function ShowErrMsg()
    alert(top.MultLang.transLang("An error occurred while accessing the NETGEAR registration server. Check your Internet connection, and then try again."));
    sessionStorage.setItem("%u", "%u");
function JsonpProcess(data)
    clearTimeout(timer);
    if(data.PingResult[0].Registered == 1)
        document.getElementById('registered').value = "2";
        document.forms[0].submit();   //post the changed value
    if(data.PingResult[0].Registered == -1)
    top.openReg();
    return true;
</script>
<body onload="RegistrationCheck()">

    xmlHttp.send(null);
    closeReg();

    closeReg();
function RegisterNow()

    webURL += "&product=%s";
    ShowWaittingMsg();
    window.open(webURL);
function ShowWaittingMsg()
    top.document.getElementById('RgsDiv').style.display="none";
    top.document.getElementById('waittingDiv').style.display="";

<script language="JavaScript">
function statusDisableOnClick()
    document.forms[0].elements.VLAN_ID_ENABLED.disabled = true;
    document.forms[0].elements.VLAN_ID_ENABLED.value = "";
    document.forms[0].elements.ROUTER_PORT.disabled = true;
    document.forms[0].elements.ROUTER_PORT.options[0].selected = true;
function statusEnableOnClick()
    var elts = document.getElementById("inputVLANID");
    if (elts)
    {
        if (elts.innerHTML == null)
        {
            document.forms[0].elements.VLAN_ID_ENABLED.disabled = true;
            document.forms[0].elements.VLAN_ID_ENABLED.value = "";
        }
        else
        {
            document.forms[0].elements.VLAN_ID_ENABLED.disabled = false;
        }
    }
    document.forms[0].elements.ROUTER_PORT.disabled = false;
</script>
</head>

<script language="JavaScript">
function getCookie(){
   var aCookie = document.cookie.split(";");
   for (var i = 0;i <aCookie.length;i++)
   {
    console.log(aCookie[i]);
   }
function selectOptions()
    var dhcp_mode = document.getElementById('dhcpMode');
	if (dhcp_mode.options[0].selected == true)
		document.forms[0].elements.refresh.disabled = true;
		document.forms[0].elements.ip_address.disabled = false;
		document.forms[0].elements.subnet_mask.disabled = false;
		document.forms[0].elements.gateway_address.disabled = false;
	else if (dhcp_mode.options[1].selected == true)
		document.forms[0].elements.refresh.disabled = false;
		document.forms[0].elements.ip_address.disabled = true;
		document.forms[0].elements.subnet_mask.disabled = true;
		document.forms[0].elements.gateway_address.disabled = true;
function dhcpModeChange()
	var dhcp_mode = document.getElementById('dhcpMode');
	if (dhcp_mode.options[0].selected == true)
		document.forms[0].elements.refresh.disabled = true;
		document.forms[0].elements.ip_address.disabled = false;
		document.forms[0].elements.subnet_mask.disabled = false;
		document.forms[0].elements.gateway_address.disabled = false;
	else if (dhcp_mode.options[1].selected == true)
		document.forms[0].elements.refresh.disabled = false;
		document.forms[0].elements.ip_address.disabled = true;
		document.forms[0].elements.subnet_mask.disabled = true;
		document.forms[0].elements.gateway_address.disabled = true;
	popUpWindown('alert','DHCP Mode','Note: Changing the protocol mode will reset the IP configuration.');
function changeRefreshVal()
	var re_fresh = document.getElementById('refresh');
	if (re_fresh.checked)
		re_fresh.value = "1";
	else
		re_fresh.value = "0";
</script>
</head>

    <script language="JavaScript">
    function checkIPv4Address(field) {
	var obj=field.value;
	var exp=/^(\d{1,2}|1\d\d|2[0-4]\d|25[0-5])\.(\d{1,2}|1\d\d|2[0-4]\d|25[0-5])\.(\d{1,2}|1\d\d|2[0-4]\d|25[0-5])\.(\d{1,2}|1\d\d|2[0-4]\d|25[0-5])$/;
	var reg = obj.match(exp);
	if(reg==null) {
		return false;
	else {
		return true;
    }
    function checkImageName(name) {
	if (name.substring(0,15)!="GS305E_loader_V") {
		return false;
        return true;
    }
    function ConfirmUpgradeFW() {
        if (checkIPv4Address(document.forms[0].ip) == 0) {
            alert ("Invalid IP Address.");
            return false;
        }
        if (checkImageName(document.forms[0].file.value) == false) {
            alert ("Invalid Bootcode Image File Name.");
            return false;
        }
        if (confirm('Please make sure bootcode image is valid,\nbecause it may cause DUT cannot boot up any more.\n\nAre you sure want to update bootcode?')) {
            return true;
        } else {
            return false;
        }
    }

<script language="JavaScript">
function changeAction(value)
	var upload_conf = document.getElementById('textfield');
	upload_conf.value = value;
	upload_conf.value = upload_conf.value.substr(upload_conf.value.lastIndexOf("\\")+1);
function checkImageName(name) {
	if (name.substring(0,15)!="GS305E_loader_V") {
		return false;
        return true;
    }
function submitBootUpdate()
    var fileDiv = document.getElementById("fileDiv");
    var p_div = document.getElementById("p_div");
    var textfield = document.getElementById("textfield").value;
    if (checkImageName(textfield) == false) {
        alert ("Invalid Bootloader Image File Name.");
        disableBtn();
        return false;
    }
	document.forms[0].submit();
	fileDiv.innerHTML="<p style='font-size:10pt; text-align:left; margin-bottom: 5px;'>Transferring bootloader...</p>" + 
	"<p style='text-align:left;'>Warning: Do not interrupt the network connection or power to the switch during this process." + 
	"Do not disconnect any Ethernet cables or power off the switch until the process is complete.</p>"
	p_div.innerHTML="<p></p>";
	disableBtn();
	return true;
function enableBtn()
	var btn_div = document.getElementById("btn_div");
	btn_div.innerHTML="<input type='button' class='buttonsOn' id='btn_Apply' value='Apply' onclick='submitBootUpdate();'>";
function disableBtn()
	var btn_div = document.getElementById("btn_div");
	btn_div.innerHTML="<input type='button' class='buttonsOff' id='btn_Apply' value='Apply' onclick='javaScript:void(0);'>";
</script>

var MultLang = {
    attrs: ["title"],
    parmMark: ["@@", "##"],
    transNodes: function(em){
        if(typeof top.lang === "undefined" || typeof top.orLang === "undefined"){
            return;
        }
        var ELEMENT_NODE = 1, TEXT_NODE = 3,
            nodeType = em.nodeType, value;
        if(nodeType === TEXT_NODE){ //translate text that is not empty
            if(!(/^\s+$/.test(em.nodeValue))){
                em.nodeValue = MultLang.transLang(em.nodeValue);
            }
        }else if(nodeType === ELEMENT_NODE){
            if(MultLang.transAttrs(em)){ //translate current element's attrs
                var childs = em.childNodes;
                for(var i=0, len=childs.length; i<len; i++){
                    arguments.callee(childs[i]); //do same operation for childNodes
                }
            }
        }
    },
    transAttrs: function(em){
        var tagName = em.nodeName.toLowerCase(),
            allAttrs = em.attributes,
            node, name, value, typ, isTrans,
            withsubtag = allAttrs.getNamedItem("withsubtag"),
            untrans = allAttrs.getNamedItem("untrans"),
            trans = allAttrs.getNamedItem("trans");
        if(!!untrans){
            return false;
        if(tagName === "script" && tagName === "style"){
            return false;
        }
        if(tagName === "input"){
            typ = em.type.toLowerCase();
            if(typ === "button" || typ === "submit" || trans){
                em.value = MultLang.transLang(em.value);
            }
        }
        for(var i=0, len=MultLang.attrs.length; i<len; i++){
            name = MultLang.attrs[i];
            node = allAttrs.getNamedItem(name);
            if(!!node){
                node.nodeValue = MultLang.transLang(node.nodeValue);
            }
        }
        if(!!withsubtag){
            em.innerHTML = MultLang.transLang(em.innerHTML);
            return false;
        }
        return true;
    },
    trim: function(str){
        return str.replace(/(^\s*)|(\s*$)/g, "");
    },
    transLang: function(str){
        var value = MultLang.trim(str);
        if(typeof top.lang === "undefined" || typeof top.orLang === "undefined"){
            return str;
        }
        if(!!top.orLang[value]){
            return top.lang[top.orLang[value]];
        }else{
            return str;
        }
    },
    transParmLang: function(str){
        var parmArr = MultLang.parmMark,
            paraNum = parmArr.length,
            dataObj = pickData(str);
        if(Object.getOwnPropertyNames(dataObj).length > 0){
            var value = dropData(str),
            tmpStr = MultLang.transLang(value);
            return addData(tmpStr);
        }
        return MultLang.transLang(str);
        function pickData(str){
            var pattern, mark, len,
                dataObj = {};
            for(var i=0; i<paraNum; i++){
                len = parmArr[i].length;
                mark = parmArr[i].substring(0, len/2);
                pattern = new RegExp(mark + '(.*)' + mark);
                if(str.match(pattern)){
                    dataObj[parmArr[i]] = str.match(pattern)[1];
                }
            }
            return dataObj;
        }
        function dropData(str){
            var mark, len,
                dataObj = pickData(str);
            for(var i=0; i<paraNum; i++){
                len = parmArr[i].length;
                mark = parmArr[i].substring(0, len/2);
                str = str.replace(mark + dataObj[parmArr[i]] + mark, mark+mark);
            }
            return str;
        }
        function addData(str){
            for(var i=0; i<paraNum; i++){
                str = str.replace(parmArr[i], dataObj[parmArr[i]]);
            }
            return str;
        }
    }
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(){
    if(!(typeof top.lang == "undefined")){
        MultLang.transNodes(document.body);
    }
    document.documentElement.style.opacity = 1;
}, false);

	str += "</span></td></tr></table></td>";
	document.write(str);
function newWindow(mypage,myname,w,h,features,purp)
	glParam = features;
	features="resizable=yes";
	var winl = (screen.width-w)/2; var wint = (screen.height-h)/2; 
	if (winl < 0) winl = 0; 
	if (wint < 0) wint = 0; 
	var settings = 'height=' + h + ','; settings += 'width=' + w + ','; settings += 'top=' + wint + ','; settings += 'left=' + winl + ','; settings += features; win = window.open(mypage,myname,settings); win.window.focus();
	if(purp=="tag"){
		document.getElementById('hd').value = glParam;
function CheckBrowser()
	var ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase(), s, o = {};  
	if( s=ua.match(/msie ([\d.]+)/) ) {  
       		 o.ie = true;  
	         o.info = "ie";  
        } else if( s=ua.match(/firefox\/([\d.]+)/) ) {  
  	     	 o.ff = true;  
           	 o.info = "ff";  
        } else if( s=ua.match(/chrome\/([\d.]+)/) ) {  
           	 o.chrome = true;  
         	 o.info = "chrome";  
        } else if( s=ua.match(/opera.([\d.]+)/) ) {  
       		o.opera = true;  
	        o.info = "opera";  
	} else if( s=ua.match(/version\/([\d.]+).*safari/) ) {  
	        o.safari = true;  
	     	o.info = "safari";  
        }  
	if( s && s[1] ) {  
	        o.version = parseFloat( s[1] );  
 	} else {  
	        o.version = 0;  
 	}  
	        o.info = (o.info?o.info:"") + "_" + o.version;
	return o;
function changeLoginButtonStyle()
	var browser = CheckBrowser();
	var docMode = document.documentMode;
	var errDiv = document.getElementById("pwdErr");
	var loginBtn = document.getElementById("loginBtn");
	if((browser.info == "ie_6") || (browser.info == "ie_7") || 
		(browser.info == "ie_8") || (browser.info == "ie_9") || 
		(browser.info == "ie_10") || (browser.info == "_0"))
		if (docMode == 7)
			if (errDiv.innerHTML != "")
			{
				loginBtn.className = "loginBtnStyle_7_2";
			}
			else
			{
				loginBtn.className = "loginBtnStyle_7";
			}
		else
			if (errDiv.innerHTML != "")
			{
				loginBtn.className = "loginBtnStyle2";
			}
			else
			{
				loginBtn.className = "loginBtnStyle";
			}
	else
		if (errDiv.innerHTML != "")
			loginBtn.className = "loginBtnStyle2";
		else
			loginBtn.className = "loginBtnStyle";
function init()
	document.getElementById('password').focus();
	window.onresize = autoResizeElement;
    	autoResizeElement();
function autoResizeElement()
    var body_height = (window.innerHeight - 2) || (document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0].offsetHeight - 6);
    document.getElementById('mainArea').setAttribute('style', 'height: '+ body_height + 'px; min-height: 768px;');
    // login container
    var loginContainerHeight = body_height - 87 - 139;
    document.getElementById('loginContainer').setAttribute('style', 'height:' + (loginContainerHeight - 93) + 'px; padding-top:95px; min-height: 454px;');
function initError()
    var err_msg = document.getElementById('err_msg').value;
    
    if (err_msg != "")
    {
        alert (err_msg);
    }
function merge(str1, str2){
    var arr1 = str1.split("");
    var arr2 = str2.split("");
    var result = "";
    var index1 = 0;
    var index2 = 0;
    while((index1 < arr1.length) || (index2 < arr2.length)){
        if(index1 < arr1.length){
            result += arr1[index1];
            index1++;
        }
        if(index2 < arr2.length){
            result += arr2[index2];
            index2++;
        }
    }
    return result;
function encryptPwd(){
    var password = document.getElementById("password").value;
    var randNum  = document.getElementById("rand").value;
    var resultStr = merge(password,randNum);
    document.getElementById("submitPwd").value = md5(resultStr);
function onEnterSub(e)
    var whKey;
    if (window.event)
    {
        whKey = e.keyCode;
    }
    else if (e.which)
    {
        whKey = e.which;
    }
    if(whKey == '13')
    {
        submitLogin();
    }
